To avoid losing entries that were actually\\n596: \\t\\t// committed, we reset Commit to max(HardState.Commit, consistent_index).\\n597: \\t\\t//\\n598: \\t\\t// See: To avoid losing entries that were actually\n\t\t// committed, we reset Commit to max(HardState.Commit, consistent_index).\n\t\t//\n\t\t// See: https://github.com/etcd-io/raft/pull/300 for more
